<Review>This shop did the diagnosis for our vehicle emissions monitors not ready issue for a reasonable price.  However, the diagnosis is incorrect.  The shop recommended us to replace the catalytic converter and the front oxygen sensor for over $2300.  Today we took our car to a Toyota dealership for a second opinion.  The dealership made all emissions monitors ready without repairing or replacing any parts.  The tecician at the dealership only did a specific Toyota drive cycle for the car. We were only charged for $155, and the car passed the smog check afterwards.  I will not take my car to this shop again for any services no matter how price competitive this shop is.  I feel that this shop technicians don't have sufficient emissions knowledge and the owner treated us like his money tree.

I want every one to know that before I took my car to this shop, my car with only about 31,600 miles was running like a brand new car.  It did not have any Diagnostic Trouble Codes (DTCs), or any Malfunction Indicator Lights (MIL) on.  Besides, this car did not show any symptoms of a bad catalytic converter or a bad oxygen sensor.  It has been running very smoothly with very good fuel economy.  I just replaced the car's battery about two months ago.  Therefore, all the previous stored OBDII emissions data was lost due to the lost of power.  I tried to drive both city streets and the freeways at various speeds without knowing exactly what the car's CAT and O2S drive cycles are required.  I could not get the CAT and the O2S monitors ready for the smog check.  Therefore the Toyota dealership I went to did exactly what I couldn't do on my own and made these two monitors ready for me.  They did not know me and I did not know them.  They did not need to clear any codes for me because there were no codes needed to be cleared.  Once they did the specific drive cycle for me, the OBD computer automatically made these emissions monitors ready.  The Toyota dealer could have lied to me and recommended some repairs or replacement of parts, so that they could have made some money off me.  But they did not because this Toyota dealer has the integrity with sufficient technical knowledge and does not cheat on its customer.  In addition, my husband and I have driven for a long time and my husband used to be a master auto mechanic. < Review>
I was impressed by the large selection of various beer types. Menu had kind of scarce variety of offerings but the food was so fresh and tasted amazing!! Staff was helpful, friendly, and attentive. They do not do taster flights but will do half pours of most beers. I had the Classic Haze (hefeweizen) and the In Lieu of Flowers (stout). Both delicious beers. Had a flatbread with goat cheese, roasted beets, pistachios, and arugula. The vinegerette on the top was the perfect addition (server told me it was made in house). Goat cheese dip was also very tasty.</Review>

I have been living here for about 2 years and I do not have any sorts of problems with this apartment besides one thing. The bottom of the doors leading outside have a small slit underneath where small critters can crawl through. I thought it was only a problem with my apartment door, but apparently other people have been experiencing this as well. These roaches come in all sizes and are freaky and scary. The staff and neighbors are nice and friendly and I have never had a problem with them. The apartments are large and spacious, but mine did not come with a plug for where the washer machine and dryer goes, so we have to hand wash, or go to places to wash them. Whenever we have a complaint, we head to the office and it is usually is fixed in less than 5 days. The neighbors and staffs are very friendly and they wave and smile to me all the time. My stuff has never been tampered with by others and this neighborhood is overall well. My only complaint are the roaches.< /review>
